{"nick":"Sorella","message":"Arnsa: it just means that you're working with lower level libraries, instead of higher-level abstractions. Node favours modular applications, which basically means you get to decide which level of abstraction is the right level for you. Sometimes lower level is what you want, sometimes you just want to worry about Doing X, but not with \"How X Gets Done\", and","date":"2016-01-20T17:43:46.736Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"Sorella","message":"for those you want a higher-level of abstraction (i.e.: something that's closer to the problem you're trying to solve).
